8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><p class="not-prose mb-2 font-medium">Update — July 10th, 2025</p><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin"><p>Zod <code>4.0.0</code> has been released on <code>npm</code>. This completes the incremental rollout process described below. To add support, bump your peer dependency to include <code>zod@^4.0.0</code>:</p><figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;peerDependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure><p>If you&#x27;d already implemented Zod 4 support according to the best practices described below (e.g. using the <code>&quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</code> subpath), then no other code changes should be necessary. This should not require a major version bump in your library.</p></div></div></div>
<p>This page is primarily intended for consumption by <em>library authors</em> who are building tooling on top of Zod.</p>
<div class="my-6 flex flex-row gap-2 rounded-lg border border-s-2 bg-fd-card p-3 text-sm text-fd-card-foreground shadow-md border-s-blue-500/50"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-info size-5 fill-blue-500 text-fd-card"><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="10"></circle><path d="M12 16v-4"></path><path d="M12 8h.01"></path></svg><div class="min-w-0 flex-1"><div class="text-fd-muted-foreground prose-no-margin">
<p>If you are a library author and think this page should include some additional guidance, please open an issue!</p>
</div></div></div>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="do-i-need-to-depend-on-zod"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=do-i-need-to-depend-on-zod">Do I need to depend on Zod?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>First things first, make sure you need to depend on Zod at all.</p>
<p>If you&#x27;re building a library that accepts user-defined schemas to perform black-box validation, you may not need to integrate with Zod specifically. Instead look into <a href="https://standardschema.dev/" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Standard Schema</a>. It&#x27;s a shared interface implemented by most popular validation libraries in the TypeScript ecosystem (see the <a href="https://standardschema.dev/#what-schema-libraries-implement-the-spec" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">full list</a>), including Zod.</p>
<p>This spec works great if you accept user-defined schemas and treat them like &quot;black box&quot; validators. Given any compliant library, you can extract inferred input/output types, validate inputs, and get back a standardized error.</p>
<p>If you need Zod specific functionality, read on.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="how-to-configure-peer-dependencies"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=how-to-configure-peer-dependencies">How to configure peer dependencies?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Any library built on top of Zod should include <code>&quot;zod&quot;</code> in <code>&quot;peerDependencies&quot;</code>. This lets your users &quot;bring their own Zod&quot;.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// package.json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;peerDependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> // the &quot;zod/v4&quot; subpath was added in 3.25.0</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>During development, you need to meet your own peer dependency requirement, to do so, add <code>&quot;zod&quot;</code> to your <code>&quot;devDependencies&quot;</code> as well.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// package.json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">  &quot;peerDependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  },</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">  &quot;devDependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">    // generally, you should develop against the latest version of Zod</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">    &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="how-to-support-zod-4"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=how-to-support-zod-4">How to support Zod 4?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>To support Zod 4, update the minimum version for your <code>&quot;zod&quot;</code> peer dependency to <code>^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// package.json</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">{</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">  &quot;peerDependencies&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">    &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">: </span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0&quot;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  }</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Starting with <code>v3.25.0</code>, the Zod 4 core package is available at the <code>&quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</code> subpath. Read the <a href="https://github.com/colinhacks/zod/issues/4371" rel="noreferrer noopener" target="_blank">Versioning in Zod 4</a> writeup for full context on this versioning approach.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Import from these subpaths only. Think of them like &quot;permalinks&quot; to their respective Zod versions. These will remain available forever.</p>
<ul>
<li><code>&quot;zod/v3&quot;</code> for Zod 3 ✅</li>
<li><code>&quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</code> for the Zod 4 Core package ✅</li>
</ul>
<p>You generally shouldn&#x27;t be importing from any other paths. The Zod Core library is a shared library that undergirds both Zod 4 Classic and Zod 4 Mini. It&#x27;s generally a bad idea to implement any functionality that is specific to one or the other. Do not import from these subpaths:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>&quot;zod&quot;</code> — ❌ In 3.x releases, this exports Zod 3. In 4.x releases, this will export Zod 4. Use the permalinks instead.</li>
<li><code>&quot;zod/v4&quot;</code> and <code>&quot;zod/v4/mini&quot;</code>— ❌ These subpaths are the homes of Zod 4 Classic and Mini, respectively. If you want your library to work with both Zod and Zod Mini, you should build against the base classes defined in <code>&quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</code>. If you reference classes from the <code>&quot;zod/v4&quot;</code> module, your library will not work with Zod Mini, and vice versa. This is extremely discouraged. Use <code>&quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</code> instead, which exports the <code>$</code>-prefixed subclasses that are extended by Zod Classic and Zod Mini. The internals of the classic &amp; mini subclasses are identical; they only differ in which helper methods they implement.</li>
</ul>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="do-i-need-to-publish-a-new-major-version"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=do-i-need-to-publish-a-new-major-version">Do I need to publish a new major version?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>No, you should not need to publish a new major version of your library to support Zod 4 (unless you are dropping support for Zod 3, which isn&#x27;t recommended).</p>
<p>You will need to bump your peer dependency to <code>^3.25.0</code>, thus your users will need to <code>npm upgrade zod</code>. But there were no breaking changes made to Zod 3 between <code><a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="6812070c285b465a5c">[email&#160;protected]</a></code> and <code><a href="/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection" class="__cf_email__" data-cfemail="1f65707b5f2c312d2a">[email&#160;protected]</a></code>; in fact, there were no code changes whatsoever. As code changes will be required on the part of your users, I do not believe this constitutes a breaking change. I recommend against publishing a new major version.</p>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="how-to-support-zod-3-and-zod-4-simultaneously"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=how-to-support-zod-3-and-zod-4-simultaneously">How to support Zod 3 and Zod 4 simultaneously?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Starting in <code>v3.25.0</code>, the package contains copies of both Zod 3 and Zod 4 at their respective subpaths. This makes it easy to support both versions simultaneously.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z3 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v3&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> Schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> =</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ZodTypeAny</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> |</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> acceptUserSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z3</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">ZodTypeAny</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> |</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // ...</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To differentiate between Zod 3 and Zod 4 schemas at runtime, check for the <code>&quot;_zod&quot;</code> property. This property is only defined on Zod 4 schemas.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" <span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> type</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>

<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="how-to-support-zod-and-zod-mini-simultaneously"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=how-to-support-zod-and-zod-mini-simultaneously">How to support Zod and Zod Mini simultaneously?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Your library code should only import from <code>&quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</code>. This sub-package defines the interfaces, classes, and utilities that are shared between Zod and Zod Mini.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// library code</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">export</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> acceptObjectSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodObject</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">){</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // parse data</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  z4.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(schema, { </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">/* somedata */</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">});</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">  // inspect internals</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">  schema._zod.def.shape;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>By building against the shared base interfaces, you can reliably support both sub-packages simultaneously. This function can accept both Zod and Zod Mini schemas.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// user code</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> { acceptObjectSchema } </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;your-library&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">acceptObjectSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ name: z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() }));</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// Zod 4 Mini</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> zm </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/mini&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">acceptObjectSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(zm.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">object</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">({ name: zm.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">() }))</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>Refer to the <a href="/packages/core">Zod Core</a> page for more information on the contents of the core sub-library.</p>
<!-- -->
<h2 class="flex scroll-m-28 flex-row items-center gap-2 undefined" id="how-to-accept-user-defined-schemas"><a data-card="" class="peer" href="?id=how-to-accept-user-defined-schemas">How to accept user-defined schemas?</a><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-link size-3.5 shrink-0 text-fd-muted-foreground opacity-0 transition-opacity peer-hover:opacity-100" aria-label="Link to section"><path d="M10 13a5 5 0 0 0 7.54.54l3-3a5 5 0 0 0-7.07-7.07l-1.72 1.71"></path><path d="M14 11a5 5 0 0 0-7.54-.54l-3 3a5 5 0 0 0 7.07 7.07l1.71-1.71"></path></svg></h2>
<p>Accepting user-defined schemas is the a fundamental operation for any library built on Zod. This section outlines the best practices for doing so.</p>
<p>When starting out, it may be tempting to write a function that accepts a Zod schema like this:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>This approach is incorrect, and limits TypeScript&#x27;s ability to properly infer the argument. No matter what you pass in, the type of <code>schema</code> will be an instance of <code>$ZodType</code>.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; $ZodType&lt;string&gt;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>This approach loses type information, namely <em>which subclass</em> the input actually is (in this case, <code>ZodString</code>). That means you can&#x27;t call any string-specific methods like <code>.min()</code> on the result of <code>inferSchema</code>. Instead, your generic parameter should extend the core Zod schema interface:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; ZodString ✅</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To constrain the input schema to a specific subclass:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// only accepts object schemas</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodObject</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To constrain the inferred output type of the input schema:</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">import</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> *</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> as</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z4 </span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">from</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF"> &quot;zod/v4/core&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">;</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// only accepts string schemas</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;&gt;(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">) {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> schema;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ✅ </span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">inferSchema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">number</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">()); </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// ❌ The types of &#x27;_zod.output&#x27; are incompatible between these types. </span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">//</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D"> // Type &#x27;number&#x27; is not assignable to type &#x27;string&#x27;</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure>
<p>To parse data with the schema, use the top-level <code>z4.parse</code>/<code>z4.safeParse</code>/<code>z4.parseAsync</code>/<code>z4.safeParseAsync</code> functions. The <code>z4.$ZodType</code> subclass has no methods on it. The usual parsing methods are implemented by Zod and Zod Mini, but are not available in Zod Core.</p>
<figure class="not-prose group fd-codeblock relative my-6 overflow-hidden rounded-lg border bg-fd-secondary/50 text-sm shiki shiki-themes github-light github-dark" style="--shiki-light:#24292e;--shiki-dark:#e1e4e8;--shiki-light-bg:#fff;--shiki-dark-bg:#24292e" tabindex="0"><button type="button" class="inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md p-2 text-sm font-medium duration-100 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 hover:bg-fd-accent hover:text-fd-accent-foreground transition-opacity group-hover:opacity-100 [&amp;_svg]:size-3.5 [@media(hover:hover)]:opacity-0 absolute right-2 top-2 z-[2] backdrop-blur-md" aria-label="Copy Text"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-check transition-transform scale-0"><path d="M20 6 9 17l-5-5"></path></svg><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-copy absolute transition-transform"><rect width="14" height="14" x="8" y="8" rx="2" ry="2"></rect><path d="M4 16c-1.1 0-2-.9-2-2V4c0-1.1.9-2 2-2h10c1.1 0 2 .9 2 2"></path></svg></button><div dir="ltr" class="overflow-hidden" style="position:relative;--radix-scroll-area-corner-width:0px;--radix-scroll-area-corner-height:0px"><style>[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]{scrollbar-width:none;-ms-overflow-style:none;-webkit-overflow-scrolling:touch;}[data-radix-scroll-area-viewport]::-webkit-scrollbar{display:none}</style><div data-radix-scroll-area-viewport="" class="size-full rounded-[inherit] max-h-[600px]" style="overflow-x:hidden;overflow-y:hidden"><div style="min-width:100%;display:table"><pre class="p-4 focus-visible:outline-none"><code><span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">function</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> parseData</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583"> extends</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">$ZodType</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt;(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">data</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#005CC5;--shiki-dark:#79B8FF"> unknown</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, </span><span style="--shiki-light:#E36209;--shiki-dark:#FFAB70">schema</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">)</span><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">:</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0"> z4</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">output</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&lt;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">T</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">&gt; {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#D73A49;--shiki-dark:#F97583">  return</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8"> z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parse</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(schema, data);</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">}</span></span>
<span class="line"> </span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">parseData</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">(</span><span style="--shiki-light:#032F62;--shiki-dark:#9ECBFF">&quot;sup&quot;</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">, z.</span><span style="--shiki-light:#6F42C1;--shiki-dark:#B392F0">string</span><span style="--shiki-light:#24292E;--shiki-dark:#E1E4E8">());</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="--shiki-light:#6A737D;--shiki-dark:#6A737D">// =&gt; string</span></span></code></pre></div></div></div></figure></div><div role="none" class="flex-1"></div><div For library authors\n\nimport { Callout } from \"fumadocs-ui/components/callout\"\n\n\u003cCallout title=\"Update — July 10th, 2025\"\u003e\n  Zod `4.0.0` has been released on `npm`. This completes the incremental rollout process described below. To add support, bump your peer dependency to include `zod@^4.0.0`:\n\n  ```json\n  // package.json\n  {\n    \"peerDependencies\": {\n      \"zod\": \"^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0\"\n    }\n  }\n  ```\n\n  If you'd already implemented Zod 4 support according to the best practices described below (e.g. using the `\"zod/v4/core\"` subpath), then no other code changes should be necessary. This should not require a major version bump in your library.\n\u003c/Callout\u003e\n\nThis page is primarily intended for consumption by *library authors* who are building tooling on top of Zod.\n\n\u003e If you are a library author and think this page should include some additional guidance, please open an issue!\n\n## Do I need to depend on Zod?\n\nFirst things first, make sure you need to depend on Zod at all.\n\nIf you're building a library that accepts user-defined schemas to perform black-box validation, you may not need to integrate with Zod specifically. Instead look into [Standard Schema](https://standardschema.dev/). It's a shared interface implemented by most popular validation libraries in the TypeScript ecosystem (see the [full list](https://standardschema.dev/#what-schema-libraries-implement-the-spec)), including Zod.\n\nThis spec works great if you accept user-defined schemas and treat them like \"black box\" validators. Given any compliant library, you can extract inferred input/output types, validate inputs, and get back a standardized error.\n\nIf you need Zod specific functionality, read on.\n\n## How to configure peer dependencies?\n\nAny library built on top of Zod should include `\"zod\"` in `\"peerDependencies\"`. This lets your users \"bring their own Zod\".\n\n```json\n// package.json\n{\n  // ...\n  \"peerDependencies\": {\n    \"zod\": \"^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0\" // the \"zod/v4\" subpath was added in 3.25.0\n  }\n}\n```\n\nDuring development, you need to meet your own peer dependency requirement, to do so, add `\"zod\"` to your `\"devDependencies\"` as well.\n\n```ts\n// package.json\n{\n  \"peerDependencies\": {\n    \"zod\": \"^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0\"\n  },\n  \"devDependencies\": {\n    // generally, you should develop against the latest version of Zod\n    \"zod\": \"^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## How to support Zod 4?\n\nTo support Zod 4, update the minimum version for your `\"zod\"` peer dependency to `^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0`.\n\n```json\n// package.json\n{\n  // ...\n  \"peerDependencies\": {\n    \"zod\": \"^3.25.0 || ^4.0.0\"\n  }\n}\n```\n\nStarting with `v3.25.0`, the Zod 4 core package is available at the `\"zod/v4/core\"` subpath. Read the [Versioning in Zod 4](https://github.com/colinhacks/zod/issues/4371) writeup for full context on this versioning approach.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n```\n\nImport from these subpaths only. Think of them like \"permalinks\" to their respective Zod versions. These will remain available forever.\n\n* `\"zod/v3\"` for Zod 3 ✅\n* `\"zod/v4/core\"` for the Zod 4 Core package ✅\n\nYou generally shouldn't be importing from any other paths. The Zod Core library is a shared library that undergirds both Zod 4 Classic and Zod 4 Mini. It's generally a bad idea to implement any functionality that is specific to one or the other. Do not import from these subpaths:\n\n* `\"zod\"` — ❌ In 3.x releases, this exports Zod 3. In 4.x releases, this will export Zod 4. Use the permalinks instead.\n* `\"zod/v4\"` and `\"zod/v4/mini\"`— ❌ These subpaths are the homes of Zod 4 Classic and Mini, respectively. If you want your library to work with both Zod and Zod Mini, you should build against the base classes defined in `\"zod/v4/core\"`. If you reference classes from the `\"zod/v4\"` module, your library will not work with Zod Mini, and vice versa. This is extremely discouraged. Use `\"zod/v4/core\"` instead, which exports the `$`-prefixed subclasses that are extended by Zod Classic and Zod Mini. The internals of the classic \u0026 mini subclasses are identical; they only differ in which helper methods they implement.\n\n## Do I need to publish a new major version?\n\nNo, you should not need to publish a new major version of your library to support Zod 4 (unless you are dropping support for Zod 3, which isn't recommended).\n\nYou will need to bump your peer dependency to `^3.25.0`, thus your users will need to `npm upgrade zod`. But there were no breaking changes made to Zod 3 between `zod@3.24` and `zod@3.25`; in fact, there were no code changes whatsoever. As code changes will be required on the part of your users, I do not believe this constitutes a breaking change. I recommend against publishing a new major version.\n\n## How to support Zod 3 and Zod 4 simultaneously?\n\nStarting in `v3.25.0`, the package contains copies of both Zod 3 and Zod 4 at their respective subpaths. This makes it easy to support both versions simultaneously.\n\n```ts\nimport * as z3 from \"zod/v3\";\nimport * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\ntype Schema = z3.ZodTypeAny | z4.$ZodType;\n\nfunction acceptUserSchema(schema: z3.ZodTypeAny | z4.$ZodType) {\n  // ...\n}\n```\n\nTo differentiate between Zod 3 and Zod 4 schemas at runtime, check for the `\"_zod\"` property. This property is only defined on Zod 4 schemas.\n\n```ts\nimport type * as z3 from \"zod/v3\";\nimport type * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\ndeclare const schema: z3.ZodTypeAny | z4.$ZodType;\n\nif (\"_zod\" in schema) {\n  schema._zod.def; // Zod 4 schema\n} else {\n  schema._def; // Zod 3 schema\n}\n```\n\n## How to support Zod and Zod Mini simultaneously?\n\nYour library code should only import from `\"zod/v4/core\"`. This sub-package defines the interfaces, classes, and utilities that are shared between Zod and Zod Mini.\n\n```ts\n// library code\nimport * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\nexport function acceptObjectSchema\u003cT extends z4.$ZodObject\u003e(schema: T){\n  // parse data\n  z4.parse(schema, { /* somedata */});\n  // inspect internals\n  schema._zod.def.shape;\n}\n```\n\nBy building against the shared base interfaces, you can reliably support both sub-packages simultaneously. This function can accept both Zod and Zod Mini schemas.\n\n```ts\n// user code\nimport { acceptObjectSchema } from \"your-library\";\n\n// Zod 4\nimport * as z from \"zod\";\nacceptObjectSchema(z.object({ name: z.string() }));\n\n// Zod 4 Mini\nimport * as zm from \"zod/mini\";\nacceptObjectSchema(zm.object({ name: zm.string() }))\n```\n\nRefer to the [Zod Core](/packages/core) page for more information on the contents of the core sub-library.\n\n{/* ### Future proofing\n\n  To future-proof your library, your code should always allow for new schema and check classes to be added in the future. The addition of a new schema type is *not* considered a breaking change. \n\n  One common pattern when introspecting Zod schemas is to write a switch statement over the set of first-party schema types:\n\n  ```ts\n  const schema = {} as z.$ZodTypes;\n  const def = schema._zod.def;\n  switch (def.type) {\n  case \"string\":\n    // ...\n    break;\n  case \"object\":\n    // ...\n    break;\n  default:\n    console.warn(`Unknown schema type: ${def.type}`);\n    // reasonable fallback behavior\n  }\n  ```\n\n  To future-proof this code, your `default` case should probably not throw an error. Instead, it should print an informative error and fall back to some reasonable behavior. If instead you `throw` an error in the default case, your library will be unusable if/when new schemas types are added in the future. Best to print a warning and treat it as a \"no-op\" (or some other reasonable fallback behavior). The same applies to unrecognized check types, string formats, etc.\n\n  */}\n\n## How to accept user-defined schemas?\n\nAccepting user-defined schemas is the a fundamental operation for any library built on Zod. This section outlines the best practices for doing so.\n\nWhen starting out, it may be tempting to write a function that accepts a Zod schema like this:\n\n```ts\nimport * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\nfunction inferSchema\u003cT\u003e(schema: z4.$ZodType\u003cT\u003e) {\n  return schema;\n}\n```\n\nThis approach is incorrect, and limits TypeScript's ability to properly infer the argument. No matter what you pass in, the type of `schema` will be an instance of `$ZodType`.\n\n```ts\ninferSchema(z.string());\n// =\u003e $ZodType\u003cstring\u003e\n```\n\nThis approach loses type information, namely *which subclass* the input actually is (in this case, `ZodString`). That means you can't call any string-specific methods like `.min()` on the result of `inferSchema`. Instead, your generic parameter should extend the core Zod schema interface:\n\n```ts\nfunction inferSchema\u003cT extends z4.$ZodType\u003e(schema: T) {\n  return schema;\n}\n\ninferSchema(z.string());\n// =\u003e ZodString ✅\n```\n\nTo constrain the input schema to a specific subclass:\n\n```ts\n\nimport * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\n// only accepts object schemas\nfunction inferSchema\u003cT extends z4.$ZodObject\u003e(schema: T) {\n  return schema;\n}\n```\n\nTo constrain the inferred output type of the input schema:\n\n```ts\n\nimport * as z4 from \"zod/v4/core\";\n\n// only accepts string schemas\nfunction inferSchema\u003cT extends z4.$ZodType\u003cstring\u003e\u003e(schema: T) {\n  return schema;\n}\n\ninferSchema(z.string()); // ✅ \n\ninferSchema(z.number()); \n// ❌ The types of '_zod.output' are incompatible between these types. \n// // Type 'number' is not assignable to type 'string'\n```\n\nTo parse data with the schema, use the top-level `z4.parse`/`z4.safeParse`/`z4.parseAsync`/`z4.safeParseAsync` functions. The `z4.$ZodType` subclass has no methods on it. The usual parsing methods are implemented by Zod and Zod Mini, but are not available in Zod Core.\n\n```ts\nfunction parseData\u003cT extends z4.$ZodType\u003e(data: unknown, schema: T): z4.output\u003cT\u003e {\n  return z.parse(schema, data);\n}\n\nparseData(\"sup\", z.string());\n// =\u003e string\n```\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"26:[\"$\",\"$L32\",null,{\"toc\":[{\"depth\":2,\"url\":\"#do-i-need-to-depend-on-zod\",\"title\":\"Do I need to depend on
